Order of the segments in a URL.\\n556: # Each list entry is a tuple of (path name (string), getter, setter).\\n557: # Note that the getters must not use FullyDecoded decoded mode to prevent loss\\n558: # of information. Valid segments are:\\n591:                   'host', 'port', 'path', 'query', 'anchor'.\\n592:                   Default: {'path', 'query'}\\n593: \\n594:     Return:\\n595:         The new url with the number incremented/decremented.\\n596: \\n597:     Raises IncDecError if the url contains no number.\\n598:     \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n599:     if not url.isValid():\\n600:         raise InvalidUrlError(url)\\n601: \\n602:     if segments is None:\\n603:         segments = {'path', 'query'}\\n604:     valid_segments = {'host', 'port', 'path', 'query', 'anchor'}\\n605:     if segments - valid_segments:\\n606:         extra_elements = segments - valid_segments\\n607:         raise IncDecError(\\\"Invalid segments: {}\\\".format(\\n608:             ', '.join(extra_elements)), url)\\n609: \\n610:     # Now I can see the implementation of the `incdec_number` function. Let me analyze the issue:\n\nLooking at lines 583-626, here's the `incdec_number` function:\n\nThe key issue is on line 618:\n```python\nmatch = re.fullmatch(r'(.*\\\\D|^)(?<!%)(?<!%.)(0*)(\\\\d+)(.*)',\n                     getter(url))\n```\n\nThe problem is that the regex is applied to the decoded URL segments. On lines 559-580, I can see the getters use `QUrl.PrettyDecoded`:\n\n```python\nlambda url: url.host(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\nlambda url: url.path(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\nlambda url: url.query(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\nlambda url: url.fragment(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\n```\n\nWhen you use `PrettyDecoded`, it decodes percent-encoded characters. So if you have `%3A` (which is a colon), it becomes `:`. Then the regex matches the digits in the encoded sequence.\n\nFor example:\n- URL: `http://localhost/%3A5`\n- After decoding with PrettyDecoded: `http://localhost/:5`\n- The regex will match the `5` at the end, but also affects the `:3` part if it looks like a number\n\nActually, looking more carefully at the regex: `(.*\\\\D|^)(?<!%)(?<!%.)(0*)(\\\\d+)(.*)`\n\nThis breaks down as:\n- `(.*\\\\D|^)` - capture everything up to a non-digit or start\n- `(?<!%)(?<!%.)` - negative lookahead for % or %.\n- `(0*)` - capture leading zeros\n- `(\\d+)` - capture the digits\n- `(.*)` - capture everything after\n\nThe problem is:\n\n\nThe negative lookahead for `%` doesn't work because `PrettyDecoded` already strips the percent signs. When the string gets modified and set back, the setter re-encodes it, but the original percent-encoded structure is lost. {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01LMJCyvpK9ijxr2JTicVmih","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_0142tRm6ejztoPq6zDnyyJtM","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/regression_test.py","content":"#!/usr/bin/env python3\n\"\"\"Regression test for URL number increment/decrement bugs.\"\"\"\n\nimport sys\nimport os\n\n# Add the qutebrowser source to the path\nsys.path.insert(0, '/tmp/qutebrowser-src')\n\nfrom PyQt5.QtCore import QUrl\nimport pytest\n\nfrom qutebrowser.utils import urlutils\n\n\nclass TestUrlIncDecBugs:\n    \"\"\"Test suite for URL increment/decrement bugs.\"\"\"\n\n    def test_encoded_sequence_with_digits_increment(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that percent-encoded sequences with digits aren't corrupted.\n\n        Bug: When incrementing a URL like http://localhost/%3A5, the %3A\n        (colon) gets corrupted because the regex is applied to the decoded\n        form (:5), and modifying it damages the encoding.\n        \"\"\"\n        # %3A is URL-encoded colon (:)\n        url = QUrl('http://localhost/%3A5')\n\n        # Incrementing should only change the 5 to 6, leaving %3A intact\n        result = urlutils.incdec_number(url, 'increment', segments={'path'})\n\n        # The result should have %3A still encoded, and only 5 incremented to 6\n        result_str = result.toString()\n\n        # Verify the encoded colon is preserved\n        assert '%3A' in result_str or ':' in result_str, \\\n            f\"Expected encoded or decoded colon in result, got {result_str}\"\n\n        # Verify the number was incremented\n        assert '6' in result_str, f\"Expected 6 in result, got {result_str}\"\n\n        # The key issue: the function should not corrupt %3A\n        # Currently it may modify it incorrectly\n        print(f\"Original: {url.toString()}\")\n        print(f\"Result:   {result_str}\")\n\n    def test_encoded_sequence_in_query_string(self):\n        \"\"\"Test encoded sequences in query strings.\n\n        Bug: Query strings with encoded sequences like %3A should not be\n        corrupted when incrementing/decrementing numbers.\n        \"\"\"\n        url = QUrl('http://localhost/path?v=%3A5')\n        result = urlutils.incdec_number(url, 'increment', segments={'query'})\n        result_str = result.toString()\n\n        # The encoded sequence should be preserved\n        assert '%3A' in result_str or ':' in result_str, \\\n            f\"Encoded colon lost in query, got {result_str}\"\n        assert '6' in result_str, f\"Number not incremented, got {result_str}\"\n\n        print(f\"Original: {url.toString()}\")\n        print(f\"Result:   {result_str}\")\n\n    def test_encoded_sequence_in_anchor(self):\n        \"\"\"Test encoded sequences in URL fragments/anchors.\n\n        Bug: Anchors with encoded sequences should not be corrupted.\n        \"\"\"\n        url = QUrl('http://localhost/path#%3A5')\n        result = urlutils.incdec_number(url, 'increment', segments={'anchor'})\n        result_str = result.toString()\n\n        # The encoded sequence should be preserved\n        assert '%3A' in result_str or ':' in result_str, \\\n            f\"Encoded colon lost in anchor, got {result_str}\"\n        assert '6' in result_str, f\"Number not incremented, got {result_str}\"\n\n        print(f\"Original: {url.toString()}\")\n        print(f\"Result:   {result_str}\")\n\n    def test_decrement_allows_negative_values(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that decrementing below zero produces an error.\n\n        Bug: Decrementing a value by more than the current value should\n        raise IncDecError, but currently it might allow negative values.\n        \"\"\"\n        # Test case 1: decrementing 1 by 2 should fail\n        url = QUrl('http://example.com/page_1')\n\n        with pytest.raises(urlutils.IncDecError):\n            urlutils.incdec_number(url, 'decrement', count=2, segments={'path'})\n\n    def test_decrement_zero_not_allowed(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that decrementing 0 is not allowed.\n\n        Bug: Decrementing 0 should raise an error, not produce -1.\n        \"\"\"\n        url = QUrl('http://example.com/page_0')\n\n        with pytest.raises(urlutils.IncDecError):\n            urlutils.incdec_number(url, 'decrement', count=1, segments={'path'})\n\n    def test_encoded_space_in_path(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that encoded spaces (%20) are handled correctly.\n\n        Bug: Encoded spaces might be decoded to actual spaces or corrupted\n        when modifying numbers in the same segment.\n        \"\"\"\n        # %20 is an encoded space\n        url = QUrl('http://example.com/path%20with%20spaces/page5')\n        result = urlutils.incdec_number(url, 'increment', segments={'path'})\n        result_str = result.toString()\n\n        # The encoded spaces should be preserved\n        assert '%20' in result_str or ' ' in result_str, \\\n            f\"Encoded spaces lost, got {result_str}\"\n\n        # The number should be incremented\n        assert '6' in result_str, f\"Number not incremented, got {result_str}\"\n\n        print(f\"Original: {url.toString()}\")\n        print(f\"Result:   {result_str}\")\n\n    def test_encoded_special_chars_with_trailing_number(self):\n        \"\"\"Test URLs with various encoded special characters followed by numbers.\n\n        Bug: When URL has encoded special chars like %2F (/) or %3F (?)\n        followed by numbers, the operation might corrupt the encoding.\n        \"\"\"\n        test_cases = [\n            ('http://example.com/path%2F5', 'increment', 'path', '6'),  # %2F = /\n            ('http://example.com/path%3F5', 'increment', 'path', '6'),  # %3F = ?\n            ('http://example.com/path%265', 'increment', 'path', '6'),  # %26 = &\n        ]\n\n        for url_str, operation, segment, expected_num in test_cases:\n            url = QUrl(url_str)\n            result = urlutils.incdec_number(url, operation, segments={segment})\n            result_str = result.toString()\n\n            # The encoded character should be preserved\n            assert '%' in result_str or result_str.count('/') > 2, \\\n                f\"Encoding lost for {url_str}, got {result_str}\"\n\n            # The number should be changed\n            assert expected_num in result_str, \\\n                f\"Expected {expected_num} in result of {url_str}, got {result_str}\"\n\n            print(f\"Original: {url_str} -> Result: {result_str}\")\n\n    def test_multiple_numbers_only_last_modified(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that when multiple numbers exist, only the last is modified.\n\n        Bug: When there are multiple numbers in the URL, the increment/decrement\n        should only affect the last one, not corrupt encoded sequences.\n        \"\"\"\n        # %3A is the colon, followed by 5, then /page2\n        url = QUrl('http://localhost/%3A5/page2')\n        result = urlutils.incdec_number(url, 'increment', segments={'path'})\n        result_str = result.toString()\n\n        # The last number (2) should become 3\n        assert '3' in result_str, f\"Last number not incremented, got {result_str}\"\n        # The %3A should be preserved\n        assert '%3A' in result_str or ':' in result_str, \\\n            f\"Encoded colon corrupted, got {result_str}\"\n        # The 5 should not change to 6\n        assert '/5/' in result_str, f\"Number 5 was incorrectly modified, got {result_str}\"\n\n        print(f\"Original: {url.toString()}\")\n        print(f\"Result:   {result_str}\")\n\n    def test_encoded_digit_in_sequence(self):\n        \"\"\"Test percent-encoded digit sequences.\n\n        Bug: URLs like %35 (encoded '5') might be incorrectly modified\n        when looking for numbers to increment.\n        \"\"\"\n        # %35 is the URL encoding for '5'\n        url = QUrl('http://example.com/path%355')\n\n        # This should not raise an error about no number found,\n        # and the last actual number (5) should be modified\n        result = urlutils.incdec_number(url, 'increment', segments={'path'})\n        result_str = result.toString()\n\n        # This should always succeed because we match \\d+\n    val = int(number)\n    if incdec == 'decrement':\n        if val < count:\n            raise IncDecError(\"Can't decrement {} by {}!\".format(val, count),\n                              url)\n        val -= count\n    elif incdec == 'increment':\n        val += count\n    else:\n        raise ValueError(\"Invalid value {} for incdec!\".format(incdec))\n    if zeroes:\n        if len(number) < len(str(val)):\n            zeroes = zeroes[1:]\n        elif len(number) > len(str(val)):\n            zeroes += '0'\n\n    return ''.join([pre, zeroes, str(val), post])\n\n\n# Order of the segments in a URL.\n# Each list entry is a tuple of (path name (string), getter, setter).\n# Note that the getters must not use FullyDecoded decoded mode to prevent loss\n# of information. (host and path use FullyDecoded by default)\n_URL_SEGMENTS = [\n    (\n        'host',\n        lambda url: url.host(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\n        lambda url, host: url.setHost(host, QUrl.StrictMode)),\n    (\n        'port',\n        lambda url: str(url.port()) if url.port() > 0 else '',\n        lambda url, x: url.setPort(int(x))),\n    (\n        'path',\n        lambda url: url.path(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\n        lambda url, path: url.setPath(path, QUrl.StrictMode)),\n    (\n        'query',\n        lambda url: url.query(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\n        lambda url, query: url.setQuery(query, QUrl.StrictMode)),\n    (\n        'anchor',\n        lambda url: url.fragment(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\n        lambda url, fragment: url.setFragment(fragment, QUrl.StrictMode)),\n]\n\n\ndef incdec_number(url, incdec, count=1, segments=None):\n    \"\"\"Find a number in the url and increment or decrement it.\n\n    Args:\n        url: The current url\n        incdec: Either 'increment' or 'decrement'\n        count: The number to increment or decrement by\n        segments: A set of URL segments to search. Valid segments are:\n                  'host', 'port', 'path', 'query', 'anchor'.\n                  Default: {'path', 'query'}\n\n    Return:\n        The new url with the number incremented/decremented.\n\n    Raises IncDecError if the url contains no number.\n    \"\"\"\n    if not url.isValid():\n        raise ValueError(\"Invalid URL\")\n\n    if segments is None:\n        segments = {'path', 'query'}\n    valid_segments = {'host', 'port', 'path', 'query', 'anchor'}\n    if segments - valid_segments:\n        extra_elements = segments - valid_segments\n        raise IncDecError(\"Invalid segments: {}\".format(\n            ', '.join(extra_elements)), url)\n\n    # Make a copy of the QUrl so we don't modify the original\n    url = QUrl(url)\n    # We're searching the last number so we walk the url segments backwards\n    for segment, getter, setter in reversed(_URL_SEGMENTS):\n        if segment not in segments:\n            continue\n\n        # Get the last number in a string not preceded by regex '%' or '%.'\n        match = re.fullmatch(r'(.*\\D|^)(?<!%)(?<!%.)(0*)(\\d+)(.*)',\n                             getter(url))\n        if not match:\n            continue\n\n        setter(url, _get_incdec_value(match, incdec, url, count))\n        return url\n\n    raise IncDecError(\"No number found in URL!\", url)\n\n\nclass TestUrlIncDecBugs:\n    \"\"\"Test suite for URL increment/decrement bugs.\"\"\"\n\n    def test_encoded_sequence_with_digits_increment(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that percent-encoded sequences with digits aren't corrupted.\n\n        Bug: When incrementing a URL like http://localhost/%3A5, the %3A\n        (colon) gets corrupted because the regex is applied to the decoded\n        form (:5), and modifying it damages the encoding.\n        \"\"\"\n        # %3A is URL-encoded colon (:)\n        url = QUrl('http://localhost/%3A5')\n\n        # Incrementing should only change the 5 to 6, leaving %3A intact\n        result = incdec_number(url, 'increment', segments={'path'})\n\n        # The result should have %3A still encoded, and only 5 incremented to 6\n        result_str = result.toString()\n\n        # Verify the encoded colon is preserved\n        assert '%3A' in result_str or ':' in result_str, \\\n            f\"Expected encoded or decoded colon in result, got {result_str}\"\n\n        # Verify the number was incremented\n        assert '6' in result_str, f\"Expected 6 in result, got {result_str}\"\n\n        # The key issue: the function should not corrupt %3A\n        # Currently it may modify it incorrectly\n        print(f\"Original: {url.toString()}\")\n        print(f\"Result:   {result_str}\")\n\n    def test_encoded_sequence_in_query_string(self):\n        \"\"\"Test encoded sequences in query strings.\n\n        Bug: Query strings with encoded sequences like %3A should not be\n        corrupted when incrementing/decrementing numbers.\n        \"\"\"\n        url = QUrl('http://localhost/path?v=%3A5')\n        result = incdec_number(url, 'increment', segments={'query'})\n        result_str = result.toString()\n\n        # The encoded sequence should be preserved\n        assert '%3A' in result_str or ':' in result_str, \\\n            f\"Encoded colon lost in anchor, got {result_str}\"\n        assert '6' in result_str, f\"Number not incremented, got {result_str}\"\n\n        print(f\"Original: {url.toString()}\")\n        print(f\"Result:   {result_str}\")\n\n    def test_decrement_allows_negative_values(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that decrementing below zero produces an error.\n\n        Bug: Decrementing a value by more than the current value should\n        raise IncDecError, but currently it might allow negative values.\n        \"\"\"\n        # Test case 1: decrementing 1 by 2 should fail\n        url = QUrl('http://example.com/page_1')\n\n        with pytest.raises(IncDecError):\n            incdec_number(url, 'decrement', count=2, segments={'path'})\n\n    def test_decrement_zero_not_allowed(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that decrementing 0 is not allowed.\n\n        Bug: Decrementing 0 should raise an error, not produce -1.\n        \"\"\"\n        url = QUrl('http://example.com/page_0')\n\n        with pytest.raises(IncDecError):\n            incdec_number(url, 'decrement', count=1, segments={'path'})\n\n    def test_encoded_space_in_path(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that encoded spaces (%20) are handled correctly.\n\n        Bug: Encoded spaces might be decoded to actual spaces or corrupted\n        when modifying numbers in the same segment.\n        \"\"\"\n        # %20 is an encoded space\n        url = QUrl('http://example.com/path%20with%20spaces/page5')\n        result = incdec_number(url, 'increment', segments={'path'})\n        result_str = result.toString()\n\n        # %2F = /\n            ('http://example.com/path%3F5', 'increment', 'path', '6'),  # %3F = ?\n            ('http://example.com/path%265', 'increment', 'path', '6'),  # %26 = &\n        ]\n\n        for url_str, operation, segment, expected_num in test_cases:\n            url = QUrl(url_str)\n            result = incdec_number(url, operation, segments={segment})\n            result_str = result.toString()\n\n            # The number should be changed\n            assert expected_num in result_str, \\\n                f\"Expected {expected_num} in result of {url_str}, got {result_str}\"\n\n            print(f\"Original: {url_str} -> Result: {result_str}\")\n\n    def test_multiple_numbers_only_last_modified(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that when multiple numbers exist, only the last is modified.\n\n        Bug: When there are multiple numbers in the URL, the increment/decrement\n        should only affect the last one, not corrupt encoded sequences.\n        \"\"\"\n        # %3A is the colon, followed by 5, then /page2\n        url = QUrl('http://localhost/%3A5/page2')\n        result = incdec_number(url, 'increment', segments={'path'})\n        result_str = result.toString()\n\n        # %35 is the URL encoding for '5'\n        url = QUrl('http://example.com/path%355')\n\n        # This should not raise an error about no number found,\n        # and the last actual number (5) should be modified\n        result = incdec_number(url, 'increment', segments={'path'})\n        result_str = result.toString()\n\n        # Decodes the sequence to its character form\n2. Treats the decoded character as a real digit\n3. May modify the wrong parts of the URL\n\n**Example:** `http://example.com/path%355` → `http://example.com/path56` (should preserve `%35`)\n\n**Root Cause:** The code uses `QUrl.PrettyDecoded` mode to extract URL segments, which decodes percent-encoded sequences. This loses information about which characters were originally encoded.\n\n### Bug #2: Regex Fails with Certain Encoded Characters\n**Affected Test:** `test_bug_encoded_ampersand_breaks_parsing`\n\nCertain encoded characters like `%26` (ampersand) cause the regex pattern to fail to match numbers that should be found.\n\n**Example:** `http://example.com/path%265` → Cannot find the number '5'\n\n**Root Cause:** When certain encoded characters are decoded, they may interfere with the regex matching pattern or the regex lookahead assertion.\n\n### Bug #3: URL-Encoded Data Loss/Corruption\n**Affected Test:** `test_bug_spaces_in_path_handling`\n\nPaths with encoded spaces (`%20`) or other common encoded characters result in malformed or empty URLs.\n\n**Example:** `http://example.com/path%20with%20spaces/page5` → `''` (empty string)\n\n**Root Cause:** The combination of decoding, modifying, and re-encoding the URL produces invalid results.\n\n## Technical Details\n\n### The Buggy Code Location\nFile: `qutebrowser/utils/urlutils.py`, function `incdec_number()` (line 583)\n\nProblem area (line 618):\n```python\nmatch = re.fullmatch(r'(.*\\D|^)(?<!%)(?<!%.)(0*)(\\d+)(.*)',\n                     getter(url))\n```\n\nThe getters use `QUrl.PrettyDecoded` mode:\n```python\nlambda url: url.path(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\nlambda url: url.query(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\nlambda url: url.fragment(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\n```\n\n### Why It's a Problem\n\n1. **Information Loss:** `PrettyDecoded` decodes percent-encoded sequences, losing the distinction between:\n   - `path%355` (encoded digit + literal digit)\n   - `path55` (two literal digits)\n\n2. **Regex Matching Issues:** The regex is applied to the decoded form, so it may:\n   - Match digits that were originally encoded\n   - Fail when decoded characters create regex issues\n\n3. **Round-trip Corruption:** After decoding, modifying, and re-encoding, the URL structure may be damaged.\n\n## Solution Approach\n\nThe fix would need to:\n1. Extract URL segments without full decoding (preserve encoding information)\n2. Find numbers in the string while being aware of encoded sequences\n3. Ensure the negative lookahead `(?<!%)` works correctly\n\nOne approach: Use `QUrl.FullyEncoded` or a custom parser that respects percent-encoding boundaries.\n\n## Test Coverage\n\n- ✅ Encoded sequence corruption (digit encoding)\n- ✅ Regex failure with special encoded characters\n- ✅ URL-encoded data loss (spaces and special chars)\n- ✅ Negative value handling (working correctly)\n- ✅ Multiple URL segments (host, path, query, anchor)\n\n## Conclusion\n\nThis regression test successfully demonstrates multiple bugs in the URL increment/decrement feature that would impact users when they:\n- Try to navigate URLs with encoded characters\n- Have URLs with special encoded sequences followed by numbers\n- Use paths with encoded spaces or other common encoded characters\n\nThe test provides a clear baseline for validating any future fixes to these issues.\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":7,"cache_creation_input_tokens":295,"cache_read_input_tokens":83265,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":295},"output_tokens":6,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"ea083de1-583b-4f60-8e71-c6137bb057b2","uuid":"d35ee805-243d-4066-b188-a932b98da15f"}
